  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=3.6)
    The story struggles to integrate its assigned elements into a cohesive narrative with meaningful stakes or character development. The elements feel like constraints the story is built around rather than organic components of a unified vision. The writing style is unnecessarily ornate, obscuring rather than illuminating meaning. Despite attempts at profundity, the story lacks the specificity and emotional authenticity needed to resonate beyond its surface-level observations about transformation and creativity.
